 In such a situation, if you wish, you can remove the smell of your shoes by adopting these measures
 1
 Avoid wearing the same shoe everyday
 do jode juute rakhen or unhen badal-badalakar pahanen
 This will allow the moisture of your sweat inside the shoes to dry and it won't stink
 2
 Put medicated in -soles inside your shoes

 3
 jab bhi baahar se lauten, juuton ko turant utaar den
 After removing the shoes, fill them with paper balls or paper

 4

 This will also dry out moisture and will not stink
 5
 If the shoes get wet then dry them with a dryer

 It is also very beneficial for those who want to lose weight, but the biggest feature of tomatoes is that even after ripening tomatoes, its nutrients remain

 2
 If the child has a dry disease, giving him a glass of tomato juice daily, it gives relief from the disease

 Ramchandra Paswan, brother of Union Minister Ram Vilas Paswan and MP from Samastipur in Bihar, died on Sunday
 vah beete kuch dinon se dilli ke ram manohar lohia aspataal main bhartee the
 He had a heart attack on 11 July
 iske baad se hi unka ram manohar lohia aspataal main ilaaj chal rahaa tha
 According to the information received, Ramchandra Paswan had complained of chest pain at night at his Delhi residence on 11 July
 iske baad hi unhen dilli ke raamamanohar lohia aspataal main bhartee karaayaa gaya tha
 Please tell that he was also kept on ventilator for the last few days
 kendriya mantri ramvilas paswan ne bhi aspataal pahunchakar unka haal-chaal liya tha
 Ramchandra Paswan defeated Congress candidate Ashok Kumar from Samastipur Lok Sabha seat in Bihar by over one lakh votes

 He is brother of Union Minister Ram Vilas Paswan

 In the Sant Nagar area of burari in the capital Delhi, many angles are coming to light with the passage of time in the death of 11 people in the same house
 parivaar kii samuhik aatmahatya ne desh bhar main logon ko sakate main daal diya he
 At the same time, many mysterious things and evidence are also found in the investigation of the case
 aisa lag rahaa he ki parivaar andhvishwaas, tantra-mantra jaisi chizon par bahut adhik yakeen karata tha or usne puri taiyaari ke saath aatmahatya kii
 Meanwhile, the crime branch source said that handwriting of younger brother Lalit, who owned a furniture shop, was taking place in both registers
 vahiin is cese main police ko ek or badi khabar haath lagi he, maut vaali raat baahar se khaane main 20 roti mangvayi gai thi
 The postmortem report disclosed, however, that the crime branch has not yet found any strong evidence of suicide
 sabhi 11 shavon kaa postmortem ho gaya he
 The postmortem report has revealed that some of the 11 people in the house were empty stomach that night
 yani us din kuch sadsy upwas par bhi ho sakate
 Because there were 11 people in the family and only 20 rotis were ordered from outside
 darasal bhaatia parivaar mahaj 15 din pehle khushiyon ke samandar main ghota laga rahaa tha
 But what happened in just 15 days that the whole family was destroyed
 jaise-jaise vakt biit rahaa or nae khulaase ho rahe hai, sawaalon kii fehrist babbti ja rahi he
 So restlessness is increasing
 kya he ek do nahin balki ek saath 11 maut kaa raaj?abhi tak police kii jaanch main kisi bhi bahari yaa 12wein shaks kii baat saamne nahin ai he
 According to forensic investigation and finger print experts, no evidence has been found of any outsider in the house, nor fingerprints of anyone other than family members
 saath hi is baat kii tasdik postmortem report main ho chuki he ki parivaar main das logon kii maut fande se jhulane se hui
 Mystery of 11 pipes behind the house? As the investigation progressed, 11 pipes were found behind the house of Bhatia family, out of which four pipes are straight and seven are bent
 dilachasp he ki pipon kii taadaad utani hi he jitani us ghar se laashen baraamad kii gai hai
 Is the whole family committing suicide in superstition? Interestingly, the investigation team has got two registers from the house, in which some things are written which raise a lot of questions
 register main likhi ek-ek baaten vaardaat se mail khaati hai
 It is written in the register that the bandages are to be tied well
 gauratlab he ki ghar se jitne shav baraamad hue unamem se ek ko chhodkar sabaki ankhon par pattiyaan bandhi thi
 It is written in the register that worship is to be done continuously after seven days
 koi ghar main aa jaae to register main likhaa he ki agle din guuruuvaar yaa ravivaar ko chune
 Interestingly, the incident took place on Sunday night
 register main likhaa he ki bebbe (daadi) khadi nahin ho saktin to alag kamare main let sakati hai
 Babey is probably said to be an elderly woman whose corpse was recovered in a separate room
 register main likhaa gaya ki maddhim roshni kaa prayog karnaa he
 It is written in the register that double the bandage of the mouth with a handkerchief
 register main likhaa gaya he ki raatri 12 se 1 ke bich kriya kerani he
 Was the whole family in a circle of tantra mantra? In the report submitted by the administration to the crime branch, it has been said that the family was very superstitious and was in the circle of tantra-mantra
 report main kaha gaya he ki parivaar kisi kitaab ke aadhaar par tantra mantra kar rahaa tha
 Was the whole family in the grip of a Baba? When the matter came to die in superstition, the investigation team ran their horses
 ab police ko ek aise baba kii talash he jisapar parivaar ko bahakaane kaa shaq he
 According to sources, the police have got Baba's clues from the mobile phone recovered from the incident
 shaq kii sooyee gum phirakar andhvishwaas main moksh prapti or jaan dene kii ore ja rahi he
 But the close of the family claims that there is neither a case of superstition nor suicide
 hatya he yaa phir andhvishwaas main di gai jaan, hakeekat jaanch puri hone ke baad hi saamne aegi

 pehali baar chaar khilaadiyon ko khel ratna puraskaar se nawaja gaya
 The credit goes to the brilliant performance of these three 'wonder Girl' at the Rio Olympics, of which Sindhu won the silver medal while Sakshi became the first Indian to win a bronze medal in women's wrestling and Deepa became the first Indian woman to qualify in gymnastics
 After winning the fourth place won the hearts of all
 jitu ne 2014 rashtramandal khelon main swarna or iesaef vishwa cap main purushon kii das meter air pistal main swarna padak jeeta tha haalanki rio olympic main vah padak nahin jeet sake 
 All of them received medals, certificates and 7 in the ceremony held at the historic Durbar Hall
 5 lakh rupye nakad puraskaar diya
 The highlight of the event, however, was female wrestler Vinesh Phogat, who was knocked out in the quarter-finals at the Rio Olympics due to a knee injury
 wheelchair par ai vinesh ko puraskaar dene raashtrapati khud aage aae or haal main maujuud logon ne taaliyon ke saath is khilaadi ke jazbe ko saraahaa

 World Health Day 2019:duniyabar main 7 april 'world health de' ke rup main manaaya jaataa he
 The World Health Organization (WHO) organizes World Health Day on 7 April every year
 iskaa uddeshy logon ko unki sehat ke prati jaagruk karnaa he
 In 1948, the WHO organized the first World Health Assembly
 iske baad saal 1950 se har 7 april ko world health de manaaya jane laga
 Under this, every year a theme related to health is chosen globally and it is tried to be applied at the global and regional level
 is saal world health de kii theme he 'universal health kawarej'
 Let us tell you some special tips to stay healthy on the occasion of World Health Day
 zyada pani pien-sehatmand rahane ke liye bharpoor maatra main pani pinaa bahut jaruri he
 The body functions properly by drinking plenty of water
 har vyakti ko dinabhar main kam se 2 litre pani jarur pinaa chahie
 Drinking water keeps the body hydrated and toxins are released from the body
 2
 Eat more fruits and vegetables - Fruits and vegetables contain plenty of vitamins, minerals and fiber
 healdi rahane ke liye dinabhar main lagbhag 5 falon kaa seven jarur karen
 Taking fruit juice in the morning breakfast is beneficial
 vahiin, snacks ke rup main seb or tarbooz aadi fal le sakate hai
 3
 diet main chini or namak kii maatra kam karen-diet main namak kaa adhik seven karne se blad pressure kii samasya hone ke saath dil kii beemaari hone kaa khatra bhi rahata he
 At the same time, sugar enhances the taste of food but causes great harm to health
 kai study main bhi is baat kii pushti ho chuki he
 Therefore, use sugar and salt in the diet to a minimum
 4
 Keep the weight under control - It is very important to keep the weight under control for a healthy lifestyle
 badha hua vajan kai gambhir bimariyon ko dastak detaa he
 These mainly increase the risk of fatal diseases like diabetes, heart attack and cancer
 isliye healdi rahane ke liye hameshaa healdi diet follow karen or apane vajan ko control main rakhen
 5
 eksrasij karen-vajan chahen kam ho yaa zyada physicli feet rahane ke liye eksrasij behad jaruri he
 Exercise burns calories
 dil sehatmand rahata he saath hi sharir kaa circulatory system thik tareeke se kaam karata he
 Exercise also strengthens muscles
 dinabhar main kam se kam 150 minute eksrasij karne kii aadat ko apane routine kaa hissaa bana len
 6
 bharpoor neend len-healdi rahane ke liye 7-8 ghante kii neend lenaa bahut jaruri he
 a good and relaxed sleep is very important for good health
 kam neend lene se sehat ko kai tarah se nuksaan pahunchataa he
 Lack of sleep is most likely to cause diabetes, stroke and obesity
 health export kaa maananaa he ki, bharpoor neend lene se dimag ko shanti milti he, pachan kriya durust rahati he
 Also, the capacity of the immune system is also fast

 vikiliks ne america ke isse sambandhit cabel ko saarvajanik kiya he

 party ke is dhade ne yah sawaal bhi kiya tha ki unhone (sanjay) desh yaa party ke liye kya yogadan kiya he
 Sanjay Gandhi was the center of attraction at the Guwahati session of the Congress and the Youth Congress Conference and was considered second nationally after his mother Indira Gandhi
 iske saath hi sanghathan ko punerjeevit karne main unki bhoomika kii bhi charchaa ho rahi thi

 Magh Purnima has special significance from religious and spiritual point of view
 is baar maaghi poornima 19 farvari ke din he
 Bathing, charity and chanting on this date are considered very virtuous
 magh poornima par magh snaan kaa vishesh mahatv bataaya gaya he
 This bath, which runs in the month of Magha, starts from the full moon of Pausha month and lasts till Magha Purnima
 magh snaan karne vaale manushyon par bhagwaan madhav prasann rahete hai tathaa unhen sukh-saubhaahgya or dhan-santan or moksh pradaan karte hai
 How to worship Sathya Narayana on Maghi Purnima - On Maghi Purnima, in the morning, bathe in a river or lake and wear clean clothes
 - snaan ke baad surya ko arghya den or pranaam karen
 - Install a photo of Lord Satya Narayan at home by laying a yellow cloth on it
 - roli mauli chaaval dhoop deep pile fal pile phool kele mishthan aadi se pujan karen or man kii ichha jarur bhagwaan ke saamne man hi man doharaaen
 - In the afternoon, after giving food to the needy people and Brahmins, give alms to Dakshina
 - daan main safed or kaale til jarur dene chahie
 In the month of Magha, perform havan with black sesame and the ancestors must be tarred
 maaghi poornima par kaise karen apane ghar main ann or dhan kii barkat-- maaghi poornima par subah uthakar snaan karen or saaf kapade pahanen tathaa maathe par kesar kaa tilak karen
 - Put Ganga water and water in a brass pot at your place of worship and light a lamp of cow's ghee
 - bhagwaan vishnu ke mantra madhusoodanay namah mantra kaa 108 baar jaap karen
 After chanting sprinkle water all over the house and in your kitchen and drink some water yourself
 - ek mitti ke diye main desi kapur jalaakar saare ghar main dikhaaen
 - By doing this you will get food and money in your house
 maaghi poornima par karen mahoupaay-- maaghi poornima par subah ke samay snaan ke jal main gangaajal daalkar snaan karen
 - Make a lamp of gram flour and fill cow's ghee in it and put four wicks of Kalave in it
 - ek done main haldi se swastik banaakar yah diya uske upar rakhen or man hi man apni ichha bolte hue yah diya kele ke ped yaa pipal ke vriksh ke neeche rakhen
 - Do this before 12:00 in the afternoon, your heart's desire will definitely be fulfilled
 police se kar report talab kar saktaa he jaanch dalbadh sakati he hero bani hyderabad police kii mushkillanushchh team ne ghatnasthal kaa muyna kiyamhila wetenry doctor ke saath darindagi ke chaar aropiyon ko hyderabad police ne shuukravaar ko encounter main maar giraaya tha
